Here's a brief description:\n\n\ud83c\udf4ePositano, Italy: A Coastal Gem\n\nNestled on the Amalfi Coast, Positano is a picturesque village, Colorful buildings cascade down cliffs, an artist's collage.\nSteep and narrow streets wind through the town, As azure waves gently kiss the shoreline down.\n\n\ud83c\udf4e\ud83c\udf4eBougainvillea blooms add bursts of vibrant hues,Amidst the whitewashed architecture, a visual muse.
